I found the issue!\n\nLooking at attrs.html line 1:\n```django\n{% for name, value in widget.attrs.items %}{% if value is not False %} {{ name }}{% if value is not True %}=\\\"{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}\\\"{% endif %}{% endif %}{% endfor %}\n```\n\nThe problem is that the attribute VALUE is being rendered in the template WITHOUT proper escaping!\n\nThe template uses `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` but this does NOT escape HTML special characters. In Django templates, the `stringformat` filter just formats the value as a string but doesn't escape it for HTML.\n\nThe issue is that while the flatatt function in Python properly escapes values using format_html, the template approach is NOT using proper escaping. The attrs are passed as a dictionary to the template, and the template renders them directly without escaping.\n\nTo fix this, we need to either:\n1. Escape the attribute values in the build_attrs method before they're passed to the template, OR\n2. While Django's template auto-escaping might help in some cases, it was not sufficient and inconsistent across different template engines (Django vs Jinja2).\n\n## Solution\nModified the `build_attrs` method to escape attribute values before returning them to the template layer:\n\n### Changes Made\n\n**File:** `django/forms/widgets.py`\n\n1. **Import addition (line 18):**\n   ```python\n   from django.utils.html import conditional_escape, format_html, html_safe\n   ```\n   Added `conditional_escape` import.\n\n2. **Method modification (lines 338-346):**\n   ```python\n   def build_attrs(self, base_attrs, extra_attrs=None):\n       \"\"\"Build an attribute dictionary.\"\"\"\n       attrs = {**base_attrs, **(extra_attrs or {})}\n       # Escape attribute values to prevent XSS and malformed HTML\n       # Boolean values and None are not escaped\n       for key, value in attrs.items():\n           if value is not None and not isinstance(value, bool):\n               attrs[key] = conditional_escape(value)\n       return attrs\n   ```\n\n## How It Works\n\n1. **Escapes regular strings:** Uses `conditional_escape()` to escape HTML special characters\n   - `\"` becomes `&quot;`\n   - `&` becomes `&amp;`\n   - `<` becomes `&lt;`\n   - `>` becomes `&gt;`\n   - `'` becomes `&#x27;`\n\n2. **Preserves safe strings:** `conditional_escape()` respects the `mark_safe()` convention\n   - Safe strings are not double-escaped\n   - Developers can still use `mark_safe()` for intentional HTML content\n\n3. **Handles special cases:**\n   - **Boolean values** (True/False): Not escaped, used as attribute presence/absence\n   - **None values**: Not escaped, omitted from output by template\n   - **SafeString values**: Not double-escaped, preserved as-is\n\n## Impact\n\n- ✅ All widget attribute values are now properly escaped\n- ✅ Prevents malformed HTML from special characters\n- ✅ Prevents XSS vulnerabilities from user-provided attributes\n- ✅ Works with both Django and Jinja2 template renderers\n- ✅ Respects mark_safe() for intentional HTML content\n- ✅ Backward compatible with existing tests and safe strings\n\n## Test Cases Validated\n\n1. ✓ Quotes in attribute values are escaped\n2. ✓ Ampersands in attribute values are escaped\n3. ✓ Angle brackets in attribute values are escaped\n4. ✓ Safe strings are not double-escaped\n5. ✓ Boolean attributes work correctly\n6. ✓ None values are handled correctly\n7. ✓ Attributes merge correctly (extra_attrs override base_attrs)\n8. ✓ Multiple special characters are all escaped\n\n## Affected Components\n\n- All widget classes (TextInput, Select, CheckboxInput, etc.)\n- All template renderers (Django and Jinja2)\n- All custom widgets that inherit from Widget\n- Widget option rendering (in choice widgets)\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":422,"cache_read_input_tokens":99187,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":422},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b77c8e1f-8300-432f-aee4-083a1ae1decc","uuid":"03f91671-34c4-4df4-98fc-c69f39506a24"}
